<span data-key="b47359c0930f4390a3ae8b5bbdff47c9"><span data-offset-key="b47359c0930f4390a3ae8b5bbdff47c9:0">Destructure an array to reference specific elements</span></span>

<span data-key="2955ee3569a84d3593b34b912a132efc"><span data-offset-key="2955ee3569a84d3593b34b912a132efc:0">\`\`\`javascript</span></span>

<span data-key="fe7ee172845046908ef1e3faecd22fbb"><span data-offset-key="fe7ee172845046908ef1e3faecd22fbb:0">let array = \[35,9\];</span></span>

<span data-key="aad0731363a24dc19129790b321f7700"><span data-offset-key="aad0731363a24dc19129790b321f7700:0">let \[firstEl, secondEl\] = array;</span></span>

<span data-key="4f7176b7fec04a94a32ecdda3ef635de"><span data-offset-key="4f7176b7fec04a94a32ecdda3ef635de:0">console.log(firstEl); // =&gt; 35</span></span>

<span data-key="e80af7c6ef5b48499bd17a2a72a10ff7"><span data-offset-key="e80af7c6ef5b48499bd17a2a72a10ff7:0">console.log(secondEl); // =&gt; 9</span></span>

<span data-key="f38670fddda942b18b1c9220454e76cb"><span data-offset-key="f38670fddda942b18b1c9220454e76cb:0">// can also destructure using ... syntax let array = \[35,9,14\]; let \[head, ...tail\] = array; console.log(head); // =&gt; 35 console.log(tail); // =&gt; \[9, 14\]</span></span>

<span data-key="5f291e725428466aa5a16dcbabc37705"><span data-offset-key="5f291e725428466aa5a16dcbabc37705:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">-</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="5f291e725428466aa5a16dcbabc37705:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> Destructure an object to reference specific values</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="4826137faa4e4adf9727386e8fd543dd"><span data-offset-key="4826137faa4e4adf9727386e8fd543dd:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="4826137faa4e4adf9727386e8fd543dd:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">-</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="4826137faa4e4adf9727386e8fd543dd:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="4826137faa4e4adf9727386e8fd543dd:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">if</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="4826137faa4e4adf9727386e8fd543dd:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> you want to use variable names that don't match the keys</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="4826137faa4e4adf9727386e8fd543dd:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">,</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="4826137faa4e4adf9727386e8fd543dd:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> you can use aliasing</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="389442a12909479aba6e791ddb124b82"><span data-offset-key="389442a12909479aba6e791ddb124b82:0">Callbacks Lesson Concepts</span></span>

<span data-key="9a0226f6cb0e4284b2700a3bfa0d6178"><span data-offset-key="9a0226f6cb0e4284b2700a3bfa0d6178:0">Given multiple plausible reasons, identify why functions are called "First Class Objects" in JavaScript.</span></span>

<span data-key="5cc759fd17b54c7cbb742b8a89de2991"><span data-offset-key="5cc759fd17b54c7cbb742b8a89de2991:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="5cc759fd17b54c7cbb742b8a89de2991:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">}</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="5cc759fd17b54c7cbb742b8a89de2991:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="3c38d45b272941c99bcc0c2644740287"><span data-offset-key="3c38d45b272941c99bcc0c2644740287:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="3c38d45b272941c99bcc0c2644740287:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">return</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="3c38d45b272941c99bcc0c2644740287:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> newArr</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="3c38d45b272941c99bcc0c2644740287:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="4dd81511a35b418f93c91877a28c672d"><span data-offset-key="4dd81511a35b418f93c91877a28c672d:0">Scope Lesson Concepts</span></span>

<span data-key="6fe6a4b58ee04595b15046ef6c914c72"><span data-offset-key="6fe6a4b58ee04595b15046ef6c914c72:0">Identify the difference between </span><span data-offset-key="6fe6a4b58ee04595b15046ef6c914c72:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">const</span></span><span data-offset-key="6fe6a4b58ee04595b15046ef6c914c72:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="6fe6a4b58ee04595b15046ef6c914c72:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="6fe6a4b58ee04595b15046ef6c914c72:4">, and </span><span data-offset-key="6fe6a4b58ee04595b15046ef6c914c72:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">var</span></span><span data-offset-key="6fe6a4b58ee04595b15046ef6c914c72:6"> declarations</span></span>

<span data-key="d39894145c164e9f9d22a5cb7e5576bd"><span data-offset-key="d39894145c164e9f9d22a5cb7e5576bd:0">Explain the difference between </span><span data-offset-key="d39894145c164e9f9d22a5cb7e5576bd:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">const</span></span><span data-offset-key="d39894145c164e9f9d22a5cb7e5576bd:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="d39894145c164e9f9d22a5cb7e5576bd:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="d39894145c164e9f9d22a5cb7e5576bd:4">, and </span><span data-offset-key="d39894145c164e9f9d22a5cb7e5576bd:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">var</span></span><span data-offset-key="d39894145c164e9f9d22a5cb7e5576bd:6"> declarations</span></span>

<span data-key="5fd7d99252b842b29c1b6a77320a677f"><span data-offset-key="5fd7d99252b842b29c1b6a77320a677f:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">var</span></span><span data-offset-key="5fd7d99252b842b29c1b6a77320a677f:1"> is function scopedâ€”so if you declare it anywhere in a function, the declaration (but not assignment) is "hoisted"</span></span>

<span data-key="27fc1de104074956aa5a3436856a5f6b"><span data-offset-key="27fc1de104074956aa5a3436856a5f6b:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">var</span></span><span data-offset-key="27fc1de104074956aa5a3436856a5f6b:1"> will also allow you to redeclare a variable, while </span><span data-offset-key="27fc1de104074956aa5a3436856a5f6b:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="27fc1de104074956aa5a3436856a5f6b:3"> or </span><span data-offset-key="27fc1de104074956aa5a3436856a5f6b:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">const</span></span><span data-offset-key="27fc1de104074956aa5a3436856a5f6b:5"> will raise a syntax error. you shouldn't be able to do that!</span></span>

<span data-key="f9cfe1e0d62e441280747babe596a8dd"><span data-offset-key="f9cfe1e0d62e441280747babe596a8dd:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">const</span></span><span data-offset-key="f9cfe1e0d62e441280747babe596a8dd:1"> won't let you reassign a variable, but if it points to a mutable object, you will still be able to change the value by mutating the object</span></span>

<span data-key="cf59a04689144f65954cc56a63aa84e0"><span data-offset-key="cf59a04689144f65954cc56a63aa84e0:0">block-scoped variables allow new variables with the same name in new scopes</span></span>

<span data-key="c914aa4262bf4a99918711995d647faf"><span data-offset-key="c914aa4262bf4a99918711995d647faf:0">block-scoped still performs hoisting of all variables within the block, but it doesn't initialize to the value of </span><span data-offset-key="c914aa4262bf4a99918711995d647faf:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">undefined</span></span><span data-offset-key="c914aa4262bf4a99918711995d647faf:2"> like </span><span data-offset-key="c914aa4262bf4a99918711995d647faf:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">var</span></span><span data-offset-key="c914aa4262bf4a99918711995d647faf:4"> does, so it throws a specific reference error if you try to access the value before it has been declared</span></span>

<span data-key="c815fc63840f44fab43a18b56f15c1b3"><span data-offset-key="c815fc63840f44fab43a18b56f15c1b3:0">if you do not use </span><span data-offset-key="c815fc63840f44fab43a18b56f15c1b3:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">var</span></span><span data-offset-key="c815fc63840f44fab43a18b56f15c1b3:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="c815fc63840f44fab43a18b56f15c1b3:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="c815fc63840f44fab43a18b56f15c1b3:4"> or </span><span data-offset-key="c815fc63840f44fab43a18b56f15c1b3:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">const</span></span><span data-offset-key="c815fc63840f44fab43a18b56f15c1b3:6"> when initializing, it will be declared as globalâ€”THIS IS BAD</span></span>

<span data-key="a3c7751626984baa8f7a5fc84c6238cf"><span data-offset-key="a3c7751626984baa8f7a5fc84c6238cf:0">Predict the evaluation of code that utilizes function scope, block scope, lexical scope, and scope chaining</span></span>

<span data-key="b4a48f5b885d4ce6b16533f3005fb842"><span data-offset-key="b4a48f5b885d4ce6b16533f3005fb842:0">scope of a program means the set of variables that are available for use within the program</span></span>

<span data-key="e5b8dc7605a5422a89fda9a52b80d857"><span data-offset-key="e5b8dc7605a5422a89fda9a52b80d857:0">global scope is represented by the </span><span data-offset-key="e5b8dc7605a5422a89fda9a52b80d857:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">window</span></span><span data-offset-key="e5b8dc7605a5422a89fda9a52b80d857:2"> object in the browser and the </span><span data-offset-key="e5b8dc7605a5422a89fda9a52b80d857:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">global</span></span><span data-offset-key="e5b8dc7605a5422a89fda9a52b80d857:4"> object in Node.js</span></span>

<span data-key="0f3a8db3d05742628cf19aab35fe7c33"><span data-offset-key="0f3a8db3d05742628cf19aab35fe7c33:0">local scope is the set of variables available for use within the function</span></span>

<span data-key="6e49ee2be69a422281c4c80ae41173e2"><span data-offset-key="6e49ee2be69a422281c4c80ae41173e2:0">for blocks (denoted by curly braces </span><span data-offset-key="6e49ee2be69a422281c4c80ae41173e2:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">{}</span></span><span data-offset-key="6e49ee2be69a422281c4c80ae41173e2:2">, as in conditionals or </span><span data-offset-key="6e49ee2be69a422281c4c80ae41173e2:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">for</span></span><span data-offset-key="6e49ee2be69a422281c4c80ae41173e2:4"> loops), variables can be block scoped</span></span>

<span data-key="d3deda625d804e9cbf416b8313f462eb"><span data-offset-key="d3deda625d804e9cbf416b8313f462eb:0">inner scope does not have access to variables in the outer scope</span></span>

<span data-key="5485ed77a49b449fac8504e922aec5ae"><span data-offset-key="5485ed77a49b449fac8504e922aec5ae:0">Define an arrow function</span></span>

<span data-key="c815e98f472f49ea94809f5bf977c23b"><span data-offset-key="c815e98f472f49ea94809f5bf977c23b:0">\`\`\`javascript</span></span>

<span data-key="43255ca12fea499095da1880c5f29fa6"><span data-offset-key="43255ca12fea499095da1880c5f29fa6:0">let arrowFunction = (param1, param2) =&gt; {</span></span>

<span data-key="4d2c89f76a4d4c93a79a3bee7068b21f"><span data-offset-key="4d2c89f76a4d4c93a79a3bee7068b21f:0">let sum = param1 + param2;</span></span>

<span data-key="89f782ea93fa40b8ab2db7ebea57819d"><span data-offset-key="89f782ea93fa40b8ab2db7ebea57819d:0">return sum;</span></span>

<span data-key="229b82ace32c44aab9abcf9bb11b0f13"><span data-offset-key="229b82ace32c44aab9abcf9bb11b0f13:0">}</span></span>

<span data-key="8d88335ec4264baf96a27b9c51ee162c"><span data-offset-key="8d88335ec4264baf96a27b9c51ee162c:0">// with 1 param you can remove parens around parameters let arrowFunction = param =&gt; { param += 1; return param; }</span></span>

<span data-key="d74ecd97d7ff4ce8a3b6020abbae5c3d"><span data-offset-key="d74ecd97d7ff4ce8a3b6020abbae5c3d:0">// if your return statement is one line, you can use implied return let arrowFunction = param =&gt; param + 1;</span></span>

<span data-key="8977a6a869444127bf49d29e665e7703"><span data-offset-key="8977a6a869444127bf49d29e665e7703:0">// you don't have to assign to variable, can be anonymous // if you never need to use it again param =&gt; param + 1;</span></span>

<span data-key="ec64cd92c7dd46e791e03ec1e6d2c5d6"><span data-offset-key="ec64cd92c7dd46e791e03ec1e6d2c5d6:0">\`\`\`</span></span>

<span data-key="a48e43d6eee2455b95a350f4b14f295b"><span data-offset-key="a48e43d6eee2455b95a350f4b14f295b:0">Given an arrow function, deduce the value of </span><span data-offset-key="a48e43d6eee2455b95a350f4b14f295b:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="a48e43d6eee2455b95a350f4b14f295b:2"> without executing the code</span></span>

<span data-key="596a25a615584d4fbfafe31f93a086c8"><span data-offset-key="596a25a615584d4fbfafe31f93a086c8:0">boundToGlobal: () =&gt; { return this.name; // this function, no matter how you call it, will be called // on the global object, and it cannot be rebound // this is because it was defined using arrow syntax },</span></span>

<span data-key="f0c94a1570084a768be74dcdd607adc4"><span data-offset-key="f0c94a1570084a768be74dcdd607adc4:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">// call unboundFunc on obj, we get "my object" console.log("unboundFunc: ", obj.unboundFunc()); // =&gt; "my object" // assign unboundFunc to a variable and call it let newFunc = obj.unboundFunc; // this newFunc will default to being called on global object console.log("newFunc: ",newFunc()); // =&gt; undefined // but you could bind it directly to a different object if you wanted console.log("newFunc: ", newFunc.bind(otherObj)()); // "my other object"</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="4547b224a9d84bff90ca95e5dd36caa8"><span data-offset-key="4547b224a9d84bff90ca95e5dd36caa8:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">// meanwhile, obj.boundToGlobal will only ever be called on global object console.log("boundToGlobal: ", obj.boundToGlobal()); //=&gt; undefined let newBoundFunc = obj.boundToGlobal; console.log("newBoundFunc: ", newBoundFunc()); // =&gt; undefined // even if you try to directly bind to another object, it won't work! console.log("newBoundFunc: ", newBoundFunc.bind(otherObj)()); // =&gt; undefined</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="657967cc1c67496b9fe98635e23186f1"><span data-offset-key="657967cc1c67496b9fe98635e23186f1:0">Javascript considers most data types to be 'primitive', these data types are immutable, and are passed by value.
